last_verified: 2026-05-16 (eighteenth session — **slice #79 Request Context tracer FULLY IMPLEMENTED; [PR #87](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/87) MERGED to `main` at `546a4b4`; issue #79 closed** from Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local. One source commit (`b40f657`, squashed into the #87 merge); no migrations; Vercel auto-deploys on merge. **What shipped**: built two new modules under `src/lib/request-context/` — (1) `evaluate-permission-rule`, the pure access-control policy (no I/O): given a rule + the caller's facts (role, granted permission keys) it returns allow/deny — `adminOnly` → admin role only, `permission` (single key or array) → admin OR holds a key, empty rule → logged-in only; (2) `withRequestContext`, the wrapper — resolves the user, the Active Organization from the `active_organization_id` JWT claim, membership role and all granted permission keys, defers the decision to `evaluate-permission-rule`, and on denial returns a standardized 401 `Not authenticated` / 403 `Permission denied` so the handler never runs; on success hands the handler a Request Context `{userId, orgId, role, supabase}`, adding the Service client only on `{serviceClient:true}`, Next.js route params passed through untouched. Converted all 6 `expenses` API routes to the wrapper and removed the inline `requireLogExpenses`: POST → `{permission:"log_expenses",serviceClient:true}` (keeps its own `user_profiles` lookup for `full_name`), PATCH/DELETE `[id]` → same rule (the submitter-or-admin ownership check stays as route business logic), the four `by-*`/`*-url` GETs → `{serviceClient:true}` logged-in-only. 37 new tests (17 pure + 8 wrapper + 12 converted-route); typecheck clean incl. Next 16's route validator; lint clean; full suite 218 green. **#80–#85 are now all unblocked** (each was blocked only by #79) and grabbable in parallel — #80 contracts+item-library, #81 invoices+estimates, #82 accounting+QuickBooks, #83 jobs+payments+payment-requests, #84 settings, #85 email+Jarvis+remaining; **#86** (delete the four old gates + publish the ungated-endpoint list) is still blocked by #80–#85. The four old gates remain in place — old + new coexist by design until #86. **Open threads**: rejection vocabulary standardized in the wrapper (`Not authenticated`/`Permission denied`); `{}` logged-in-only routes now run 2 extra auth queries (perf out of scope per #78); the expenses `by-*`/`*-url` GETs read with the Service client without org-scoping — a pre-existing data-scoping gap flagged for the #86 follow-up; `src/lib/email/sync-folder-incremental.test.ts` still carries the pre-existing unrelated `TS2322`. Per `feedback_pause_between_issues.md` the #80–#85 batches are reviewed and paused between. See handoff [[2026-05-16-79-request-context-tracer-shipped]].)

(2) Picked **candidate #1** and grilled it (`/grill-me`). **Design decisions locked**: (a) the module hands back a full context bundle `{userId, orgId, role, supabase}`, not a yes/no gate; (b) **User client** always, **Service client** opt-in only via `serviceClient:true`; (c) one function `withRequestContext` with a settings-object rule — `{permission:"key"}` / `{permission:[...]}` / `{adminOnly:true}` / `{}`; (d) **wrapper style** — an endpoint is handed to `withRequestContext`, so on denial the wrapper sends the rejection and the handler never runs (the deny-check cannot be forgotten); (e) **behavior-preserving conversion** — gated routes map 1:1, ungated routes wrapped logged-in-only, and the work *produces a list* of ungated endpoints for a separate triage follow-up (no access rules tightened in #78); (f) build the module first, then convert in feature-area batches, delete the four old gates last (old+new coexist meanwhile). (3) Created **`CONTEXT.md`** at the repo root — the project's first code-domain glossary, defining **Organization**, **Active Organization**, **Request Context**, **User client**, **Service client**. (4) Filed PRD **issue #78** (`ready-for-agent`) — modules `evaluate-permission-rule` (pure decision function) + `withRequestContext` (wrapper); all three test layers selected (pure / wrapper / converted routes). (5) Ran `/to-issues` — broke #78 into **8 slice issues**, all `ready-for-agent`: **#79** (HITL, no blockers) builds both modules + all three test suites + converts the `expenses` routes as the tracer; **#80–#85** (AFK, each blocked by #79) are conversion batches — #80 contracts+item-library, #81 invoices+estimates, #82 accounting+QuickBooks, #83 jobs+payments+payment-requests, #84 settings, #85 email+Jarvis+remaining; **#86** (AFK, blocked by #80–#85) deletes the four old gates and publishes the ungated-endpoint list. **What's next**: #79 is the only unblocked issue — implement it next; on merge #80–#85 become grabbable in parallel. Per `feedback_pause_between_issues.md` the issues were filed not started. **Open threads**: ungated `settings/*`+`payments/*` endpoints are known potential security gaps — #78 wraps them logged-in-only (no behavior change), #86 produces the list, tightening is a deliberate separate follow-up; the pre-existing soft-archive `DELETE /api/settings/contract-templates/[id]` gap (no `requirePermission`+org filter) will surface in the #84 ungated list; `src/lib/email/sync-folder-incremental.test.ts` still carries the pre-existing unrelated `TS2322` error. Also still queued, untouched: **#58 umbrella** has #62+#63 `ready-for-agent`; the **#68 real-email demo** remains on Eric's plate. The remaining 6 architecture candidates (email-send consolidation, QB sync processor, contract auto-fill orchestration, EstimateBuilder money math, the async-action component pattern, payment-request validation) are a ready backlog for future `/improve-codebase-architecture` follow-ups. **Mechanical state**: branch `main`, HEAD `3cab99e`, no source commits, no migrations, no Vercel deploy; working tree carries new `CONTEXT.md` + the `00-NOW.md` edit + this session's handoff file, plus gitignored `out/` — all to be committed and pushed to `main` per Eric's request. **Memories**: none saved this session. last_verified: 2026-05-15 (fifteenth session — **exploratory/planning: contract-template permanent-delete design grilled to shared understanding and filed as PRD [issue #76](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/76), `ready-for-agent`. No source commits** from Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local. `main` HEAD unchanged at `4632045`. **What this session produced**: (1) brought `00-NOW.md` current — it had silently fallen four sessions behind (frontmatter still read "twelfth session — #66 drag-to-pan"); the fourteenth-session entry below was added covering #69 + #70 + PRD #65 fully delivered, and the thirteenth-session #69 entry was never separately stamped (it lives in [[2026-05-14-69-form-builder-safety-net-shipped]] and is rolled into the fourteenth entry). (2) Grilled (`/grill-me`) and filed (`/to-prd`) **issue #76 — "Permanently delete contract templates"**: a `⋯`-menu "Delete permanently" action that hard-removes a contract template and its uploaded PDF. **Four user-facing decisions locked by Eric**: (a) delete is **blocked only while a customer is mid-signing** — a template referenced by a `sent`/`viewed` contract is protected; every other case (including templates with a history of signed contracts) is deletable, because a signed contract is already its own stamped PDF; (b) unsent `draft` contracts **cascade-delete** with the template (confirm dialog discloses the count); (c) an already-`signed` contract's original signing link **still serves its stamped `signed_pdf_path`** after the template is gone (graceful degradation in `build-public-signing-view.ts`); (d) **one-step UI** — "Delete permanently" lives directly in the templates-list `⋯` menu with a confirmation popup, no archive-first two-step. **Technical shape in the PRD**: FK migration on `contracts.template_id` (drop `NOT NULL`, FK → `ON DELETE SET NULL`, so `Contract.template_id` type becomes `string | null`); a new `hard_delete_contract_template(p_template_id, p_org_id)` Postgres RPC (raise-if-blocked, delete drafts, delete template — authoritative re-check at delete time); a new `DELETE /api/settings/contract-templates/[id]/permanent` route (gated + org-scoped, best-effort storage cleanup of `pdf_storage_path`); a new advisory `GET …/[id]/usage` route feeding the confirm/block dialog its counts; graceful-degradation edits to `build-public-signing-view.ts` + `sign/[token]` + `in-person` routes. **Deep module**: `template-deletion-eligibility` — pure function, input the referencing contracts as `{id,status}`, output `{deletable, blockers, draftIds}`, build first via `/tdd`. **Tests** (Eric selected all four): the eligibility module, the RPC, the usage endpoint, the signing-view degradation. **Open threads from this session**: the FK migration is unwritten — per `feedback_supabase_mcp_prod_migration_approval.md` its SQL must be surfaced for a plain-text "yes apply" before `apply_migration`; the pre-existing soft-archive `DELETE /api/settings/contract-templates/[id]` (the "Archive" action) lacks both `requirePermission` and an org filter — the PRD explicitly leaves that as-is and notes tightening it as a separate follow-up. **What's next**: issue #76 is `ready-for-agent` and self-contained — an AFK agent or the next session can implement straight from it (suggested order: FK migration → eligibility module → RPC → routes → signing-view degradation → list UI). Per `feedback_pause_between_issues.md` it was filed but not started. Also still queued, untouched this session: **#58 umbrella** has #62 (Restore voided) + #63 (Permanently delete voided) `ready-for-agent`; the **#68 real-email demo** remains on Eric's plate. **Mechanical state**: branch `main`, HEAD `4632045`, no source commits, no migrations, no Vercel deploy; working tree carries only the `00-NOW.md` edit + this session's handoff file, plus gitignored `out/`. **Memories**: none saved this session. See [[2026-05-15-76-template-hard-delete-prd]].)

last_verified: 2026-05-14 (twelfth session — **#66 drag-to-pan shipped, PR open, browser smoke PASSED on AAA prod localhost** from Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local. One source commit `a9b07a5` on branch `claude/66-drag-to-pan`, opened as **[PR #73](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/73)** against `main`; smoke-results comment posted; awaiting Eric's merge. Three files, +109 / −2. **What shipped**: `<main>` scroll container in `template-pdf-editor.tsx` now binds `onPointerDown` that records `startX/Y` + `startScrollLeft/Top`, then window-attaches `pointermove`/`pointerup`/`pointercancel`. `pointermove` activates panning only after `isPanThresholdExceeded(dx,dy) >= 4px hypot`, then sets `scrollLeft = start - dx`, `scrollTop = start - dy`. `pointerup` sets `suppressClickRef.current = true` with `setTimeout(0)` fallback clear so the trailing synthesized click doesn't deselect a previously selected field. Handler gates on `panEnabled = zoom > 1`; below that, only the prior click-to-deselect runs and scrollbars/trackpad pan natively. Cursor: `cursor-grab` class on `<main>` when `panEnabled`, plus `document.body.style.cursor = "grabbing"` during active pan via `useEffect([panning])` so the cursor stays consistent if drag crosses chips. Threshold helper extracted to `src/lib/contracts/pan-threshold.ts` with 6 unit tests; the rest is DOM glue per the issue's note. **Interference-free**: chips' `onPointerDown` already `stopPropagation`s (chip drag + resize bypass the pan handler); palette HTML5 drop uses `dragstart`/`dragover`/`drop` on a separate event stream from `pointerdown`. **Tests**: **123/123 green** (+6 new) via `npx vitest run`; `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on changed files (preexisting unrelated `sync-folder-incremental.test.ts:246` error from #64 work remains, verified against `main`). **Browser smoke against AAA prod** on template `ec9b8c74...` after Eric pasted anon + service-role keys (initially asked only for anon — discovered `/pdf` route needs service-role to mint signed URLs, fixed mid-smoke). Plus: drag-end suppress-click works (selected chip stayed selected after pan-drag). **Smoke results posted as [PR #73 comment](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/73#issuecomment-4453431035)** with the six-AC table inline. `.env.local` deleted post-smoke; no creds persisted. **#68 status**: PR #72 was already merged at session start (HEAD `0165cc0` on main); `gh issue close 68` rejected with "already closed" — `Closes #68` auto-closed it. Pre-#67 the SELECT pulled only string columns by name so the bug was hidden. **Fix**: `String()`-coerce non-null `row[column]` in `merge-field-resolver.ts:160-167` before `applyOptionLabel`. **Two more bugs caught while in the same file**: (A) `fetchLatestFormConfig` in `merge-fields.ts:70-80` had no `organization_id` filter — sign page uses `createServiceClient()` (RLS-bypassed), so on multi-org installs it grabbed the global-max-version row (Test Company v103 instead of AAA v5). `buildMergeFieldValues` now fetches `jobs.organization_id` first and threads it through. Takes a narrow `RestoreTargetInputs` interface (3 nullable timestamps) so any row shape — full Contract, list-view row, hand-built fixture — can be passed without ceremony. 5 tests cover all four branches plus the precedence edge case (all three timestamps non-null → 'signed' wins). **Route**: brand-new `POST /api/contracts/[id]/restore` at `src/app/api/contracts/[id]/restore/route.ts` — auth → load contract (404 if missing) → status guard (`!== 'voided'` → 409 for draft/sent/viewed/signed/expired) → `rpc('restore_contract', { p_contract_id, p_restored_by: user.id })` → 500 on error → 200. **No payment-block check** (restore is the opposite of destruction); **no storage surface** (slice #60's sidecar pattern means the canonical signed PDF is always clean — happy-path test positively asserts `storageDownloads.length === 0 && storageUploads.length === 0` even on a signed-then-voided contract). **RPC**: new `restore_contract(p_contract_id uuid, p_restored_by uuid)` mirrors build59's `void_contract` style — DECLARE v_org/v_job_id/v_signed_at/v_first_viewed_at/v_sent_at/v_target + RAISE-on-missing guard; derives v_target via the same precedence as the TS pure function (single-source via a PG function exposed to JS was considered and rejected since the TS function needs to run in the browser for future UI optimism); `UPDATE contracts SET status=v_target, voided_at=NULL, voided_by=NULL, void_reason=NULL WHERE id=… AND status='voided'` (Eric explicitly chose to clear these — audit trail lives in `contract_events` rows, not on the contracts row); RAISE if NOT FOUND; INSERT `contract_events` with `organization_id=v_org`, `event_type='restored'`, `metadata=jsonb_build_object('restored_by', p_restored_by, 'target_status', v_target)`; recompute `jobs.has_pending_contract`. **Migration**: also ALTERs `contract_events.event_type` CHECK to accept `'restored'`. **Critical discovery during prep**: the live CHECK constraint includes **14 values beyond what the build33 source file shows** — paid/payment_failed/refunded/partially_refunded/dispute_opened/dispute_closed/estimate_sent/invoice_sent/estimate_trashed/estimate_restored/estimate_purged/invoice_trashed/invoice_restored/invoice_purged — these were added by post-build33 migrations not captured in any `supabase/migration-build*.sql` source file. The build68b migration explicitly preserves all of them plus adds `'restored'`. 2026-05-13 (evening — **void/restore/permanently-delete PRD published** on Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local, third session of the day after the morning design+spec+#57-publish and the afternoon #57-implement. **Standalone design-only session — zero source commits; one artifact: GitHub issue [#58](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/58) `Feature: void / restore / permanently delete contracts from the job view` with `ready-for-agent` label, published via `/to-prd` after a 9-question `/grill-me` session.** **The user-visible bug**: today's `…` menu in `src/components/contracts/contracts-section.tsx:69-75` registers a `mousedown` doc-listener to close the menu, but the menu panel only stops `onClick`, so `mousedown` on a menu item closes the menu before the click event lands — visible symptom is "tap Discard/Void, menu disappears, nothing happens." One-line fix during implementation (switch listener to `click`, or stop `onMouseDown` propagation). **The deeper redesign** (the actual reason for the grill) introduces a two-tier lifecycle: `alive → void → restore-or-permanently-delete`, with **drafts shortcut to one-click hard-delete** (no void tombstone for failed-send leftovers). **Nine grilled decisions**: (1) **hard-delete, not soft-delete** — `DELETE FROM contracts WHERE id = ?` with cascades to `contract_signers`+`contract_events` already in place from build-33 (`migration-build33-contracts.sql:54,77`); rejected `deleted_at` tombstone column per `no real customers yet`; (2) **signed-PDF watermark goes to a sidecar path** (`${signed_pdf_path}.voided.pdf` or sibling) so the canonical signed PDF is untouched on void and restore is trivially clean; today's `void/route.ts:69-92` overwrite-at-same-key bug becomes the fix; zero existing voided-signed prod rows so no backfill; (3) **restore target status derived from preserved timestamps** (`signed_at` → `signed`; else `first_viewed_at` → `viewed`; else `sent_at` → `sent`; else `draft`) — no new `voided_from_status` column; (4) **payment-block applied to void AND permanent-delete, NOT restore** — permanent-delete re-runs the check at delete time (covers void-before-payment / payment-after-void case); extract today's inline check (`void/route.ts:46-66`) to a shared `assertJobHasNoPayments(supabase, jobId)` helper; (5) **drafts get a one-click hard-delete shortcut** — menu on draft row says "Delete draft" not "Discard draft", single confirmation, direct DELETE, no void step; (6) **light confirmation on permanent-delete** ("Are you sure? This can't be undone." Cancel/Delete) — no type-the-title or admin gate; rationale: already 2 clicks deep, payment-block catches worst footgun, solo user with no real customers; (7) **all three actions silent** — no automatic emails to signer on void/restore/delete; `build-public-signing-view.ts:156,209` already returns HTTP 410 on voided contracts so link-going-dead is enough signal; (8) **both Restore + Permanently delete behind the `…` menu** on voided rows (remove the `{!isVoided && ...}` gate at line 404); (9) **no confirmation on Restore** — one click → toast. **Module sketch confirmed**: 3 routes (`POST void` modified, `POST restore` new, `DELETE` new with status-branching), 2 new RPCs (`restore_contract`, `delete_contract`), 1 new event type (`'restored'` added to `ContractEventType`), 3 deep extractions (`computeRestoreTargetStatus` pure, `assertJobHasNoPayments` shared, `writeVoidWatermarkSidecar` extracts the inline overwrite). **Test scope: option C (full coverage)** — pure unit tests for `computeRestoreTargetStatus` (4 branches + edge cases) + restore-route integration tests (draft/sent/viewed/signed targets, signed-PDF preservation, audit row insert, has_pending_contract recompute, 404/409/401) + delete-route integration tests (draft no-payment-check path, voided with-payment-check path, sidecar+canonical storage cleanup, has_pending_contract recompute, 409s on alive contracts, 404/401) + void-route sidecar-behavior tests (watermark lands on sidecar key, canonical untouched, plus existing scenarios continue passing). Pattern lifts the in-file Supabase fake from `src/lib/contracts/finalize.test.ts:170-300` (commit `83b5312`, this morning) — kept inline in each new test file per the "premature extraction is its own anti-pattern" rule from #57's spec, until a third consumer needs it. **Mechanical state at session end**: branch `main` HEAD `693c5fd` unchanged (zero source commits this session), in sync with `origin/main`; working tree clean except gitignored `out/`; this handoff write becomes a single vault commit + push; no migrations, no Vercel deploys (docs-only), no TestFlight pushes. **GitHub state**: issue #58 OPEN with `ready-for-agent` label; the canonical five-label triage vocabulary applies as-is. **Memories saved this session**: none — decisions live in #58 + this handoff. **Open threads (none are #57 regressions, none are #58 work)**: durable secondary audit-write fallback (still ~Build 67); manual email-resend flow (still no design); `@testing-library/react` install for mobile tests (pre-existing); TestFlight push (Apple Dev Program enrolled, still deferred); portrait-lock Info.plist Xcode rebuild from `63bc89e`; Finding-B regression test (airplane-mode untested); 65b.1 follow-up list (~6 items); Step 5 Supabase email templates; AAA QB sandbox token (expired 2026-04-21); 67c2 reviewer F4-F8; 5xx redactor sweep across ~80 routes. **Implement-#58 is the natural next-session candidate** — mirrors the #57 flow (`/orient` → open issue → `/tdd` vertical slices → single commit → close issue with commit pointer). **Decoupling note**: the mousedown one-line fix could ship on its own ahead of the full #58 implementation if the user wants the buttons working before the full lifecycle redesign lands. 2026-05-13 (afternoon — **finalize refactor IMPLEMENTED** on Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local, second session of the day after the morning design+spec). **Single source commit `83b5312` `refactor(contracts): harden finalize — idempotency, error-checked flip, unified audit rows` landed on `main`; issue #57 closed.** Implemented via `/tdd` skill with vertical-slice cycles. Per the morning handoff's open question, **chose option (b)**: no build card — issue #57 + `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-13-finalize-signed-contract-refactor-design.md` are the durable record. **Three fixes (matching spec)**: (1) **idempotency early-return** — `finalizeSignedContract` reads `contracts.status` + `signed_pdf_path` from DB as its first action; if `status === 'signed'` returns `{ signedPdfPath: <existing>, wasAlreadyFinalized: true, notifications: emptyNotifications() }` immediately (no re-stamp, no re-flip, no emails); (2) **error-checked status flip** — closes the 15h-deferred silent-failure bug; the `contracts.update(...)` now captures `{ error }` and throws via `sealContract`, so emails never dispatch on a failed seal; (3) **unified audit-row metadata** — every intended recipient produces one `contract_events` row with `sent: {kind, signer_id?, provider, message_id}` / `failed: {kind, signer_id?, error}` / `skipped: {kind, signer_id?, skipped_reason}` (reason ∈ `settings_missing | no_internal_recipient | no_signer_email`); audit-write failures fall back to structured `console.error("[finalize] audit row write failed", {contractId, kind, signerId, originalOutcome, auditError})` per `project_no_real_customers_yet.md` (durable secondary fallback explicitly deferred). **Internal structure**: `finalizeSignedContract` is now a ~25-line orchestrator over two private helpers — `sealContract` (transactional, throws on any failure, returns `{ signedPdfPath, stampedPdfBytes }`) and `dispatchNotifications` (best-effort, never throws out, returns the structured outcomes block). Plus a `recordOutcome(supabase, contractId, outcome)` helper that translates each outcome into the unified row metadata. **New return shape**: `{ signedPdfPath, wasAlreadyFinalized, notifications: { summary: {sent, failed, skipped}, outcomes: Array<{recipient, signerId?, to, result}> } }`. **Callers updated** (`/api/sign/[token]/route.ts`, `/api/contracts/in-person/route.ts`): both capture `finalizeResult` and `console.warn` the summary when `summary.failed > 0 || summary.skipped > 0`; **HTTP response shape unchanged**. **Test file** `src/lib/contracts/finalize.test.ts` (new, 783 lines) with an in-file Supabase fake scoped to exactly what finalize touches (no general-purpose mock pulled in — chain-builder over `.from(...).select.eq.limit.maybeSingle`, `.update.eq`, `.insert`, plus `storage.from(...).download/upload`; tracks every insert/update/upload). External deps mocked at module level (`./stamp-pdf`, `./resolve-merge-values`, `./email-merge-fields`, `./email`). **Seven tests, all 6 spec scenarios + happy path**: idempotency-no-op / status-flip-error-throws / happy-path-return-shape / mixed-outcome-dispatch / settings-missing / no-internal-recipient-resolved / signer-with-empty-email. **Test infra gotchas surfaced**: `NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL` must be `vi.stubEnv`'d in `beforeAll` because `appUrl()` is called for the internal-email `contract_platform_url` merge value; `vi.clearAllMocks()` clears call history but **preserves implementations**, so a top-level `beforeEach` re-stamps the email-module mocks each test (defaults: `sendContractEmail → resend/msg-stub`, `resolveInternalRecipient → "internal@example.com"`). **TDD flow** ran vertical (RED→GREEN per cycle): idempotency → status-flip-error → happy-path return-shape (the big rewrite — extracted helpers, defined outcome types) → mixed/skipped/null scenarios passed on first run after the structural rewrite. Diverged from the spec's "step 8: write tests last" — TDD puts tests first by definition. **Test results**: 7/7 finalize tests pass; **27/27 full repo** (one pre-existing transform failure in `src/lib/mobile/use-capture-mode.test.ts` for missing `@testing-library/react` is **unrelated** to this work — predates this session). `tsc --noEmit` clean on all touched files; `eslint` clean on all touched files. **Mechanical state at session end**: branch `main` HEAD `83b5312`, **one commit ahead of `origin/main` `9fb246d` at handoff write-time** (this session's source commit is local — the user's `/handoff` arg `then commit +push+merge` means this handoff vault commit + the source commit get pushed as a single sequence after the diff is shown); working tree clean except gitignored `out/`; **no migrations** (`contract_events.metadata` is `jsonb`, no schema change); **no Vercel deploy yet** (auto-triggers on push; server-side fix only, no UI changes); **no TestFlight**. **GitHub state**: **issue #57 closed** with implementation summary comment pointing at commit `83b5312`. No PR opened (work landed on main directly, matching morning pattern). **Memories saved this session**: none — decisions live in the spec + this handoff. **Open threads (none are finalize regressions)**: durable secondary audit-write fallback filed for ~Build 67 (when `no_real_customers_yet` no longer holds); manual email-resend flow out-of-scope for #57 (audit log is today's recovery surface); `@testing-library/react` install whenever next session touches mobile tests (pre-existing); TestFlight push (Apple Dev Program enrolled, still deferred); portrait-lock Info.plist Xcode rebuild from `63bc89e`; Finding-B regression test (airplane-mode untested); 65b.1 follow-up list (~6 items); Step 5 Supabase email templates; AAA QB sandbox token (expired 2026-04-21); 67c2 reviewer F4-F8; 5xx redactor sweep across ~80 routes. **Next-session smoke surface**: the next contract signed in prod is the production smoke for this refactor — worth watching the first prod signing event in Vercel logs to confirm `notifications.summary` warn-log doesn't fire on the happy path and that the new audit-row metadata shape lands as expected. **Reusable pattern note**: the in-file Supabase fake at `finalize.test.ts:170-300` is the first of its kind in this repo (prior tests fake localStorage or exercise pure helpers); if a second test consumer needs a Supabase fake, lift this chain-builder pattern — premature extraction is its own anti-pattern. Picked #2 (`contracts/finalize.ts`) over #1 (highest dev-experience leverage) because contract signing is the load-bearing product surface and the `no real customers yet` window is the cheap moment to fix audit-trail integrity before ESIGN/UETA forensics becomes load-bearing. Grilled the design through six decisions: (1) **one function** (`finalizeSignedContract`), same callers, internal-only restructuring; (2) **refuse-to-run-twice idempotency** by reading `contracts.status` first and returning `wasAlreadyFinalized: true` on retry — "smart partial-retry recovery" explicitly cut, manual resend is a future flow; (3) **error-checked `contracts.update(...)`** so the silent status-flip failure deferred from 15h's reviewer findings gets fixed in the same change; (4) **internal split into two private helpers** (`sealContract` transactional + throws, `dispatchNotifications` best-effort + never throws out); (5) **audit-row shape: medium** — one `contract_events` row per intended recipient with unified outcome shape (`sent: {kind, signer_id?, provider, message_id}` / `failed: {kind, signer_id?, error}` / `skipped: {kind, signer_id?, skipped_reason}` where reason ∈ `settings_missing | no_internal_recipient | no_signer_email`), plus `console.error` to Vercel logs when `writeContractEvent` itself fails; durable secondary fallback (separate table or structured-logging pipeline) explicitly deferred per `project_no_real_customers_yet.md`; (6) **richer return shape** `{ signedPdfPath, wasAlreadyFinalized, notifications: { summary: {sent, failed, skipped}, outcomes: Array<{recipient, signerId?, to, result}> } }`; "already signed" returns normal result not exception. Spec lives at `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-13-finalize-signed-contract-refactor-design.md` with eight-step work order — **steps 1-2 (idempotency check + error-checked update) are load-bearing safety fixes that could ship as their own commit**. Six tests listed (status-flip failure throws / already-signed no-op / mixed-outcome dispatch / settings missing produces all-skipped rows / internal-unresolvable / signer-with-null-email) — all impossible against today's code. **GitHub issue [#57](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/57) `Refactor: harden contract finalize` published via `/to-prd` with new `ready-for-agent` label (created this session, color `0E8A16`)**. **Mechanical state at session end**: branch `main` HEAD `5c105e3`, in sync with `origin/main`; two commits this session on top of `aa879b6` (the 65b.2 merge); working tree clean except gitignored `out/` (this vault commit will be a third commit on top); no migrations, no Vercel deploys (docs-only), no TestFlight push. **Memories saved this session**: none — design decisions live in the spec + handoff, which is the right home. **Open threads inherited (none are 65b.2 regressions)**: **implement #57 / the finalize refactor** is the natural next-session candidate; TestFlight push (Apple Dev Program enrolled, still deferred); portrait-lock Info.plist Xcode rebuild from `63bc89e`; Finding-B regression test (red pulsing dot on real upload failure); 65b.1 follow-up list (~6 items); Step 5 Supabase email templates; AAA QB sandbox token (expired 2026-04-21); 67c2 reviewer F4-F8; 5xx redactor sweep across ~80 routes. 2026-05-11 (build 65b.2 FINAL POLISH + READY TO MERGE on Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local — third session of the day after the morning spec+plan and the afternoon execute+redesign. **7 polish commits `b2d3e70..5b00253`; PR #53 status MERGEABLE at https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/53; Vercel + Vercel Preview Comments green; Eric signed off ("looks good") and requested the merge.** Phase 1 — **resolved the open coord-space mystery from the prior handoff** (bottom corners square + camera bleeding above status bar). Read the iOS plugin source directly: `CameraPreviewPlugin.swift:92-93` divides incoming `x`/`y` by `UIScreen.main.scale` (asymmetric — width/height NOT divided), and `previewView` is added to `webView.superview` at iOS UIWindow coords (origin = screen top including status bar), while our `getBoundingClientRect` returned CSS coords offset below the status bar by Capacitor's `contentInset:'automatic'` — combined ~47pt drift explained both bugs. **The fix is a design pivot, not a coord patch**: `7f96090` rewrote the layout so the camera viewport is FULL-WIDTH and FLUSH to the screen top (iOS status bar overlays directly on the live preview), with only the BOTTOM corners rounded. Native rect math collapses to `x=0, y=0` + `height = cssHeight + safeAreaTop` — x/y=0 makes the plugin's scale-division a no-op, and the safe-area-top probe (transient CSS div with `height: env(safe-area-inset-top)`) extends the native rect upward to cover the status-bar area so the CSS-wrapper's bottom corner masks land exactly on the camera's hard bottom edge. Top icons (X/flip/flash/mode/settings) became absolute overlays on the camera in this commit. Smoke confirmed both bugs gone on iPhone. Forward-compatible — the in-pass Task 3 web fix wasn't time-pressured because the column default makes existing web uploads produce correct rows immediately. **Reviewer-driven amend in Task 5:** code-quality reviewer caught a `cachedKey` value-cache race where two concurrent first-call `encrypt()`s could each generate a key and clobber each other in iOS Keychain (any data encrypted with the losing key would be unrecoverable). Fix: cache the **promise**, not the resolved key — `keyPromise: Promise<CryptoKey> | null` + `loadOrGenerateKey()` returns the import-key result directly + `.catch` resets the cache for retry. Third vitest case `concurrent encrypt calls share a single key (no race)` locks this in. **One in-bundle scope-creep fix in Task 6:** `camera-view.tsx:151` had a `const sidecar: CaptureSidecar = { ... }` literal annotation that broke against the now-stricter `CaptureSidecar` type — removed the explicit annotation (1-character fix; lets TS infer the literal as `WritableSidecar`-compatible). **Beneficial deviations from plan-snippets:** Task 3 + Task 10 use `.maybeSingle()` instead of `.single()` for `user_profiles.full_name` lookup (matches existing pattern in `src/lib/auth-context.tsx:62-66` and aligns with spec's stated defensive-fallback intent — `.single()` would throw on missing profile and break the upload, defeating the spec). Task 1's first vitest-config attempt over-engineered with `@vitejs/plugin-react`, `resolve.alias`, and dropped `include`/`exclude` — caught at controller-level diff inspection, amended to match plan byte-for-byte (no `.tsx` tests in the plan; alias unneeded for colocated tests). Task 10 implementer caught a missing `@capacitor/app` dep (not in plan) and `npm install`ed it (`@capacitor/app@8.1.0`); also added `if (!user || !orgId) return` guard so the worker never constructs with a null org (because `getActiveOrganizationId` returns `string | null`). **Test suite at session end:** 3 files / 12 tests passing — `crypto-vault` (3: roundtrip + IV-randomness + concurrent-no-race), `exif-read` (2: known fixture + non-JPEG fallback), `upload-queue` (7: 4 backoff-math + 3 stale-claim-recovery). **Mechanical state:** local `main` HEAD `9afbc55` (Task 0 docs commit, **1 commit ahead of `origin/main` at `2259dfe`** — not pushed); local `build-65c-upload-pipeline` HEAD `22f9297`, **never pushed to origin** (no `origin/build-65c-upload-pipeline` ref exists). `build-65c-upload-pipeline` was branched off `9afbc55` (so pushing the feature branch will also force-include the Task 0 docs commit). Working tree clean except `?? out/`; no Vercel deploys triggered; no TestFlight pushes; 0 memories saved this session. **Subagent-driven-development pattern observations:** dispatch implementer subagent (haiku for mechanical 1-2-file edits, sonnet for tasks involving design judgment or larger codebases), independently verify the resulting commit by reading the diff before dispatching reviewers, dispatch spec-compliance review, then code-quality review for non-trivial changes; reviewer-found Important issues fed back to the implementer for amend. 2026-05-07 (build 15h SPEC + PLAN session on Vanessa's MacBook Pro: design + 11-task implementation plan written for the second slice of the 25b carve-out from 15d (first slice was 15e's next-signer-handoff). Spec `71f6aed` at `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-07-build-15h-post-sign-confirmation-emails-design.md` (376 lines); plan `c0b4011` at `docs/superpowers/plans/2026-05-07-build-15h-post-sign-confirmation-emails.md` (981 lines). No implementation this session — fresh session needed to execute the 11 tasks. **Scope: customer + internal post-sign confirmation emails with the signed PDF attached, on both `POST /api/sign/[token]` (remote emailed-link flow) and `POST /api/contracts/in-person` (iPad in-person flow), via a new shared `finalizeSignedContract` helper at `src/lib/contracts/finalize.ts` that owns stamp + upload + status flip + email dispatch + audit rows.** Helper extraction collapses ~60 lines of duplicated stamp pipeline currently inlined in both routes into a single call site; adds ~80 lines of email dispatch (one customer email per signer with `signer_id` audit metadata + provider/message_id on success; one internal email to `resolveInternalRecipient`; best-effort with per-email try/catch isolation so one bad signer email never blocks the others). Plus orphan deletion: `src/app/api/contracts/[id]/sign/route.ts` (475 lines, no callers since 15d), `src/app/api/contracts/[id]/regenerate-pdf/route.ts` (100 lines, no callers), `src/lib/contracts/pdf.ts` (685 lines, only consumer was the two orphan routes) — total ~1,260 lines removed — plus the dead `package.json` postinstall step that copies `pdf.worker.min.mjs` into `/public/` (replaced by 15e's bundler-resolved `new URL("pdfjs-dist/build/pdf.worker.min.mjs", import.meta.url)` in `configure-pdfjs.ts`) + the `/public/pdf.worker.min.mjs` artifact itself. **Major decision locked: NO regenerate-PDF endpoint.** Original brainstorm proposed 4 items including "regenerate signed PDF" (re-stamp an already-signed contract using current code/data — would have replaced the orphan endpoint). Eric questioned legality. Determined: editing a signed legal artifact is content modification under ESIGN/UETA; safe path for a bad PDF is **void + re-sign** (matches DocuSign / HelloSign). Orphan `regenerate-pdf/route.ts` deleted with no replacement. An earlier intermediate brainstorm decision ("fresh re-resolve of merge values on regenerate") was identified as carrying its own legal risk (a corrected job typo would silently change the saved signed PDF) and is moot now. Lesson preserved: never re-derive signed-contract content from current state; treat signed PDFs as immutable. Other decisions locked: in-person flow sends same emails as remote (industry standard), every signer gets their own customer-confirmation email (homeowner+spouse pattern, not just primary signer), internal email goes to reply-to fallback (`eric@aaacontracting.com` for AAA's Resend setup), best-effort emails so signing always succeeds even on email failure, audit on success captures `provider` + `message_id` (symmetrizes with 15e's failure-only audit shape), shared helper not duplicated code. Plan structure: T1 pre-flight DB check (verify `contract_email_settings.signed_confirmation_*_template` cols populated for AAA + Test Co), T2 helper file alone (commit; no callers yet), T3 wire both routes (commit + push; deploys live), T4 deploy verification, T5–T7 three live smoke tests against AAA prod (remote / in-person / failure-path with corrupted signer-2 email and audit-row checks via Supabase MCP), T8 test-data cleanup with `SET LOCAL storage.allow_delete_query='true'` admin escape, T9 orphan deletion (separate commit so reversible), T10 postinstall + `/public/` worker cleanup, T11 final tsc/build/push + handoff. Subagent-driven execution recommended for the 11 tasks. `main` HEAD `c0b4011` 2 commits ahead of `origin/main` at session end (spec `71f6aed` + plan `c0b4011`); session-start pulled `0c3f16e..14edb05` from origin (PR #49 zoom controls on PDF template editor merged earlier today by Eric, separate from 15h). Same bug exists at `regenerate-pdf/route.ts:59` and legacy `[id]/sign/route.ts:338` but those are deferred-to-25b orphans, not in the active 15d flow. **Bug 5 — `signature_upload_failed: mime type image/png is not supported`:** `contract-pdfs` bucket allowed_mime_types was set to `['application/pdf']` only when the bucket was created in Tasks 1–9; signature PNG upload at `/api/sign/[token]/route.ts:178` (`upload(sigPath, sigBytes, {contentType: "image/png", upsert: true})`) was rejected with this error from Supabase Storage. Fix: migration `build15d_signature_png_mime_fix` applied via `mcp__claude_ai_Supabase__apply_migration`: `UPDATE storage.buckets SET allowed_mime_types = ARRAY['application/pdf', 'image/png'] WHERE id = 'contract-pdfs'`. [[contracts-builder]] **Slice #70 (auto-fill checkboxes) SHIPPED to branch `claude/70-autofill-checkboxes` 2026-05-14 (fourteenth session). [PR #75](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/75) OPEN against `main` awaiting Eric's merge.** Two source commits: `ae6affb` `contracts: auto-fill checkboxes bound to intake merge fields (#70)` + smoke-driven fix `d1cd5f5` `contracts: auto-fill evaluator must use raw merge values not labels (#70 smoke fix)`. **What shipped**: a checkbox overlay can be configured as either "Customer ticks at signing" (today's behavior) or "Auto-fill from intake data" — auto-fill checkboxes bind to a merge slug (from the #67 registry) plus a list of match values, and at contract draft creation each is ticked iff the job's resolved value is in `matchValues`. Auto-filled checkboxes are non-interactive (disabled) at signing and customers can't toggle them. New pure `auto-checkbox-evaluator.ts` module (12 truth-table tests); two new validator error codes (`unknown_autofill_merge_field`, `empty_autofill_match_values`) with 6 tests; new `GET /api/contracts/preflight?jobId=&templateId=` returning the list of auto-bound checkboxes whose source slug resolves to null so `send-contract-modal` warns before send. Both `POST /api/contracts/send` and `POST /api/contracts/in-person/start` fetch overlay_fields, compute `evaluateAutoCheckboxes(overlay_fields, buildMergeFieldRawValues(...))`, and patch `contracts.customer_inputs` post-RPC (the existing `create_contract_with_signers` RPC has no customer_inputs param — patch separately, no migration). `PublicSigningView` gained `customer_inputs`; signer view filters auto-bound checkboxes out of the interactive overlay and renders them as `<input disabled checked>`. `requiredMissing` (client) and the server `missing` checks both defensively skip auto-fill checkboxes. Inspector grew a "Checkbox type" radio toggle in `field-inspector.tsx` with `CheckboxInspectorBody` + `AutoFillBindingEditor` — pill-typed merge fields show option labels next to raw values; storing happens on raw option values; an amber inline warning flags `matchValues` entries that aren't in the bound field's option set (non-blocking per spec). Auto-fill checkboxes get an auto-generated `inputKey` (e.g. `auto_a3f9b1cd`) so `customer_inputs` + the existing `stampPdf` path keep working with zero changes — the inputKey field is hidden in the UI per spec. **Mid-smoke bug + fix**: the first send attempt produced `customer_inputs.auto_residential_70 = false` even though `property_type=single_family` matched the binding. Root cause: `resolveMergeFieldValues` applies `applyOptionLabel` to pill-typed fields by default, so `buildMergeFieldValues` returned `"Single Family"` (label) while `matchValues` stores `"single_family"` (raw value). Equality match never fired. Fix: added `opts.rawValues` flag to `resolveMergeFieldValues` that skips `applyOptionLabel` + `LEGACY_TITLECASE_COLUMNS` title-case; new `buildMergeFieldRawValues` wrapper sets it; the three call sites (send / in-person start / preflight) switched to the raw variant. Labeled values were never correct for equality-match evaluation — they're only for display/stamping. Plus a regression test in `auto-checkbox-evaluator.test.ts` (`"matches against raw option values, not display labels"`) that pins this contract with both cases. **All 11 spec ACs PASS** end-to-end against AAA prod via the Vercel PR preview on Untitled Template (6) `ec9b8c74…` and job WTR-2026-0016 `27de9daa…` (Eric Daniels, property_type=single_family). DOM probe confirmed AC6/AC7: auto-fill checkbox `{aria:"Auto-filled checkbox", disabled:true, checked:true}`, customer-ticks checkbox `{disabled:false, checked:false}`. **Bonus smoke**: end-to-end sign + stamped-PDF visual proof — POSTed `/api/sign/[token]` with a 1×1 PNG, contract flipped `sent → signed`, `customer_inputs` merged to `{auto_residential_70: true, agreed_terms_70: true}`, opened the stamped PDF inline via `URL.createObjectURL` + `<embed>` — both X glyphs visible at (100, 700) and (200, 700) on page 1. Tests: **156/156 green** (138 baseline + 18 new across 2 files); `tsc --noEmit` clean on changed surface; preexisting `sync-folder-incremental.test.ts:246` error from #64 work remains. Smoke results posted as two [PR #75 comments](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/75#issuecomment-4454659558). No migrations applied (JSONB-only schema extension on `OverlayField`). **Smoke fixtures left on Untitled Template (6)**: two test checkboxes at PDF coords (100, 700) and (200, 700) on page 1 — `auto_residential_70` (auto-fill, bound to property_type ∈ {single_family, multi_family, condo}) + `agreed_terms_70` (customer-ticks "I agree to the terms"). Useful for future smoke runs; Eric can delete via the inspector. **PRD #65 contracts-template-builder is fully delivered pending PR #75 merge** — slices #66 (drag-to-pan), #67 (dynamic merge fields), #68 (email pickers), #69 (form-builder safety net), and #70 (auto-fill checkboxes) all shipped. **Per `feedback_pause_between_issues.md`: pause for review/approval before any next initiative.** Next session resumption point: confirm Eric merged + Vercel auto-deploys + #70 auto-closes. **New this session**: `buildMergeFieldRawValues` vs `buildMergeFieldValues` is the load-bearing split — raw for equality-matching against `matchValues`, labeled for display/stamping; the regression test pins this contract directly. **Open threads carried**: #69 follow-up `unknownMatches` warning is informational-only; #68 real-email demo still on Eric; cross-org caution if `buildMergeFieldValues` called with non-existent jobId; preview-route `SAMPLE_MERGE_VALUES` still on legacy field names. [PR #74](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/74) merged, issue #69 auto-closed.** Three protections against silent breakage of contract/email templates when an intake field is renamed/redirected/deleted: (1) `TemplateReferenceLookup` module (`src/lib/contracts/template-reference-lookup.ts`) with pure `extractReferencedSlugs(overlay_fields)` + `buildReferenceIndex(templates, slugs)` (9 unit tests) and RLS-scoped `findReferencingTemplates(supabase, slugs)` returning `{ slug: [{ id, name, is_active }] }`; (2) server-side delete guard via `form-config-removal-guard.ts` (6 unit tests) wired into both `POST /api/settings/intake-form` and `POST /api/settings/intake-form/restore` — diffs prior vs new config, returns 409 with structured `blocked` array when a removed field's slug is referenced; (3) new `GET /api/settings/intake-form/usage` endpoint returning the same map for every slug derived from the active org's latest form_config. [[build-15h-followup]] **Chrome `/sign/[token]` hang — email-iframe sandbox inheritance fix — SHIPPED 2026-05-08.** Closes finding #4 (final 15h-deferred UX item) — Chrome rendering `/sign/[token]` as a stuck "Loading PDF…" shell while Safari rendered fine. Single-commit fix `d9f92ef` on `main`, pushed to `origin/main`. One-line edit at `src/components/email-reader.tsx:62`: `sandbox="allow-same-origin allow-popups"` → `sandbox="allow-same-origin allow-popups allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox"`. **Root cause:** the in-app `/email` inbox renders email body HTML inside `<iframe sandbox="allow-same-origin allow-popups">` with `<base target="_blank">` injected so every link opens a new tab. Per HTML spec, popups opened from a sandboxed iframe inherit the parent's sandbox flag set unless `allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox` is also granted; inheritance carried `allow-scripts`'s absence into the new tab → React/Next/pdfjs scripts blocked at parse time → SSR shell rendered (header + "Loading PDF…" + footer) but never hydrated → no PDF fetch ever attempted. Console signature: 28× "Blocked script execution because document's frame is sandboxed and the 'allow-scripts' permission is not set." Same exact error signature 15e fixed for a different cause (pdf.js fake-worker fallback iframe was sandboxed); this time the parent tab itself was sandboxed via inheritance — the cause was upstream. **Diagnosis was the work; the fix was one token.** Three-context repro nailed it: incognito-paste rendered, MCP-controlled tab in same regular Chrome profile rendered (`navigator.serviceWorker.getRegistrations() = []`, `caches.keys() = []`, `pdfjs.GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc = "/_next/static/media/pdf.worker.min.0wghn0~9oxou6.mjs"`, zero console errors), but click-from-email in regular Chrome still hung — differentiator was the navigation path, not the URL or the cache or login state. Eric's initial hypothesis ("logged in on Chrome but not on Safari?") was checked and ruled out via four-bullet falsification: `/sign/[token]` is in the `src/proxy.ts:48` public-page allowlist, SSR uses `createServiceClient` not user session, the PDF fetch goes to a Supabase signed URL on a different origin so app-domain cookies don't follow, and the pdfjs worker is served from `_next/static/media/...` (matcher-exempt). Login state was not the differentiator. Live AAA-prod verification PASS via Eric clicking the contract link from `/email` after Vercel deploy — verbatim "it worked." `npx tsc --noEmit` clean; no build verified (single-token edit, zero type or runtime risk; Vercel auto-deployed). **Customer impact:** real but narrow — only customers whose email client renders the body inside a sandboxed iframe (Gmail web, Outlook web, the in-app `/email` inbox) hit this; native mail clients (Apple Mail, Outlook desktop, mobile mail apps) don't sandbox the rendered body so most real-world signing flows would not have hit this. **All four 15h UX findings now closed.** Memorized the linkage to project memory `project_email_iframe_sandbox_popups.md` so future sandbox-tightening on `<EmailBodyFrame>` doesn't re-break signing — `allow-scripts` MUST stay omitted on the iframe itself (email bodies must not execute scripts), `allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox` is the only correct way to break the inheritance chain. Diagnosis fully controller-driven via `mcp__claude-in-chrome__*` (one `browser_batch` call combining `javascript_tool` + `read_console_messages` + `read_network_requests` was decisive); zero subagents this session. See [[2026-05-08-build-15h-followup-chrome-sign-sandbox]].

I have to hard close the app to be able to get back into the platform." Two fixes landed in-session: `631750e` `<DownloadPdfButton>` client component intercepts the click only when `display-mode: standalone` matches OR `navigator.standalone === true`, fetches PDF as blob, calls `navigator.share({ files: [file] })` → iOS Share Sheet → Save to Files (PWA stays alive, no inline preview detour); falls back to blob-URL synthetic-click if `canShare({ files })` is false; final last-ditch `window.location.href`. Added `window.Capacitor?.isNativePlatform?.() === true` to the OR condition. **No native plugin install required:** iPadOS 16.4+ supports Web Share with files inside WKWebView natively, plain web `navigator.share({ files })` works without `@capacitor/share`. **No new TestFlight build needed for the fix** — `capacitor.config.ts:9` sets `server.url = 'https://aaaplatform.vercel.app'` so the iPad TestFlight app is a thin WKWebView loading live Vercel content; web changes propagate on next app launch. [[merge-field-pills]] **Email-template merge-field pills — MERGED to `main` 2026-05-08 18:06:05 UTC, deployed to prod.** UI polish on top of the 15-series email-template editors: merge fields render as styled purple pills inline with body text + subject line in both Settings → Contracts and Settings → Payments; selector dropdown shows plain-English labels ("Customer Name") with raw `{{token}}` preserved on hover via `title` attribute; pills are atomic Tiptap nodes (backspace deletes whole pill); unknown tokens (e.g. user-typed `{{not_a_real_field}}`) render in a red warning style; signing_link picker still inserts an `<a href="{{signing_link}}">Open document</a>` anchor in the body (recipients see "Open document" rather than the raw URL; for the subject it goes in as a regular pill since `<input>`-equivalents can't hold an anchor). Single commit `1d95462` `feat(email-templates): merge-field pills in subject + body editors` on `claude/bold-shamir-638769` (10 files / +1484 / -220), shipped via [PR #50](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/aaa-platform/pull/50) merged into `main` at 2026-05-08 18:06:05 UTC (merge commit `ad6b296`). Vercel preview confirmed working by Eric pre-merge at https://aaaplatform-git-claude-bo-89a564-aaa-disaster-recovery-e5661f28.vercel.app; Vercel auto-deployed to production on merge. **Implementation:** three new files — `src/components/contracts/merge-field-node.ts` (Tiptap atomic Node extension parsing + emitting `<span data-field-name="x" class="merge-field-pill">{{x}}</span>`; sets `data-unknown="true"` when the field doesn't resolve to any known merge field), `src/components/contracts/tokenize-for-editor.ts` (DOM-walking pre-processor that wraps bare `{{token}}` text in pill spans on load — idempotent via parent-`data-field-name` skip; doesn't touch attribute-embedded tokens like `href="{{signing_link}}"` because the walker only visits text nodes), `src/components/contracts/merge-field-input.tsx` (single-line pill-aware contenteditable for the Subject — Tiptap with Document/Paragraph/Text/History only, Enter suppressed via `handleKeyDown`, serializes pill nodes back to `{{token}}` strings via custom walker so the saved subject stays a plain string and the DB contract is preserved). Plus four modified: `tiptap-editor.tsx` (accepts optional `extraExtensions` + `onReady(editor)` props; tokenizes incoming `content` before mount), `email-template-field.tsx` + `payment-email-template-field.tsx` (full rewrites using the new components + label-driven dropdown picker; payments threads payment-specific names through `extraResolvableNames` so payment tokens don't render as warning pills), `globals.css` (warning-style + `merge-field-input-line` single-line-input rules). Four Tiptap sub-extensions added: `@tiptap/extension-document/paragraph/text/history` (npm caret resolved to ^3.23.1; existing pkgs are ^3.22.2 — minor version skew, build passes; `@tiptap/core` got bumped via peer deps). Resolver-side **zero changes** — `lib/contracts/merge-fields.ts:228` and `lib/contracts/email-merge-fields.ts:81` already handled both `<span data-field-name="x">{{x}}</span>` and bare `{{x}}` shapes (per 15h-followup), so this is purely additive UI. **Subagent-driven-development for execution:** 9 tasks × (implementer + spec reviewer + code-quality reviewer) + 1 final cross-task review = ~28 subagent invocations, all passes ✅ on first iteration thanks to plan grilling at design time (most implementer tasks ran on haiku since the plan provided code verbatim; sonnet reserved for Tasks 3/4/6/7 which involved cross-file integration). [[build-15h-followup]] **Clickable signing_link anchor — SHIPPED 2026-05-07.** First of the four 15h-deferred UX findings closed. Single commit `2f3160e` `fix(contracts): always render {{signing_link}} as a clickable anchor` on `main`, pushed to `origin/main` (one file, +48/-1). Edit confined to `src/lib/contracts/email-merge-fields.ts`: added `escapeAttr` + `escapeText` helpers and a `substituteSigningLink(html, url)` pre-pass that runs against the body before `applyMergeFieldValues`. Three regex passes handle the three saved-body shapes — (1) `<a href="{{signing_link}}">Open document</a>` (seeded default from `migration-build33-contracts.sql:445`) → fills the href in place, preserves the visible "Open document" text; (2) `<span data-field-name="signing_link">…</span>` (Tiptap pill) → replaces the span with a fresh `<a href="URL">URL</a>`; (3) bare `{{signing_link}}` in body content (the case Eric kept hitting where the saved body had lost its anchor wrapper) → wraps in `<a href="URL">URL</a>`. Guarded with `if (extras.signing_link)` so `finalize.ts:155`/`:207` empty-link calls (post-sign customer/internal confirmation emails) are no-ops. `resolveEmailTemplate` is the choke point so the fix automatically applies to all four email-sending paths: `POST /api/contracts/send`, `POST /api/contracts/[id]/resend`, `POST /api/sign/[token]` (15e next-signer handoff), and `src/lib/contracts/reminders.ts` (cron-driven reminders). **Tiptap config not touched** — read of `node_modules/@tiptap/extension-link/dist/index.js:190-207` confirmed default `isAllowedUri` regex's `[^a-z]` branch matches `{` (so `{{signing_link}}` *should* survive editor round-trip); substitution-layer fix is the recovery path regardless of whether the saved body actually loses the anchor. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean, `npm run build` ✓ Compiled in 14.2s. Vercel auto-deployed; Eric ran a real prod send and confirmed verbatim: "Okay it works. It now creates a clickable link." Three of four 15h UX findings still open: View PDF iPad→Safari unauthorized, Download PDF dead-end viewer, Chrome `/sign/[token]` loading-screen hang. See [[2026-05-07-build-15h-followup-signing-link-anchor]].

[[build-15f]] + [[build-15g]] **Signature pad Type mode + send-body signing_link guard-rail — FULLY SHIPPED 2026-05-07.** Two tightly-coupled sub-builds that landed in a single session on top of 15d. **15f** rewrites `src/components/contracts/signature-pad-modal.tsx` (123 → 234 lines, single-file change) — bumps draw stroke `lineWidth` 2 → 3.5 + adds `lineJoin = "round"` + replaces per-pointer `lineTo + stroke` with quadratic-curve midpoint smoothing (standard `signature_pad`-library pattern, eliminates polyline kinks at the heavier weight); adds a Type tab (text input + 200px live HTML preview rendered in **Caveat** Google font via `next/font/google` mirroring `Inter` in `app/layout.tsx:2`) that on Insert renders the typed name onto an offscreen 600×200 canvas via `ctx.fillText` with auto-shrink-to-fit (60 → 28px floor at 4px steps until `measureText.width < 560`) and exports PNG via `toDataURL("image/png")` — **zero backend change** because both tabs emit through the existing `onConfirm(dataUrl: string)` contract and the server-side `stamp-pdf.ts` + `/api/sign/[token]` POST + pdf-lib stamping path is byte-identical regardless of which tab sourced the PNG; adds a shared disclaimer footer ("I understand this is a legal representation of my signature." — exact HelloSign verbatim, ESIGN-aligned, no checkbox per industry norm) with Cancel + Insert buttons (Confirm renamed Insert). Tab a11y wired with `role="tablist"` / `role="tab"` / `aria-selected` / `aria-controls`. Font-load race guarded by `await document.fonts.load("60px Caveat")` before the offscreen render + a pre-warm on modal open. Tab-switch preserves both states (typed text + drawn ink); canvas re-initializes on each return to Draw because preserving `<canvas>` state inside a `hidden` tabpanel was deemed fragile and out of scope. Sole caller `contract-signer-view.tsx:219` unchanged. Spec at `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-07-signature-pad-type-mode-design.md` (commit `669996d`); 3-task plan at `docs/superpowers/plans/2026-05-07-signature-pad-type-mode.md` (commit `fdfdcd0`); feat commit `9852ee4`. **15g** is a guard-rail surfaced during 15f end-to-end smoke when Eric replaced the default email body with the literal string `TESTINGGGGGGG` for a test send — Resend accepted dispatch (contract `6a9eaac0-1825-4297-b96d-65915c97ae38`, message_id `89306a36-e156-4d49-8a0e-01f8c61187e3`), Eric received the email, but it had no link to sign. Root cause: server-side `applyMergeFieldValues` in `src/lib/contracts/merge-fields.ts:211` is a **substitution-only** resolver — replaces existing tokens but never prepends missing ones; body lacked `{{signing_link}}` → resolver had nothing to substitute → email rendered as just the test text. Two-layer fix in commit `a1dfb06`: **server** at `src/app/api/contracts/send/route.ts` rejects HTTP 400 when the request body lacks `{{signing_link}}` (accepts either `{{double_brace}}` or the Tiptap pill form `data-field-name="signing_link"`, matching what the resolver recognizes; error copy "Email body must contain the {{signing_link}} placeholder so the recipient gets a sign-in link."); **client** at `src/components/contracts/send-contract-modal.tsx` derives `bodyHasSigningLink` using the same regex/contains check, renders an inline red warning under the body editor when the user has typed something but lacks the token, and disables the Send button while the token is missing (submit-time toast as final fallback). End-to-end verified against prod Vercel: SendContract modal correctly disabled Send when body was blanked, restoring `{{signing_link}}` re-enabled it, fresh contract sent + email arrived w/ working link, signing page opened the new tabbed modal, both Draw + Type tabs produced PNGs that were stamped onto the contract PDF, auto-shrink + tab-switch preservation + disclaimer copy all PASS. **Signing URL recovery technique discovered:** when a contract goes out with a broken email body but the row is in DB with a valid `link_token`, `SELECT link_token FROM contracts WHERE id = '<id>'` via Supabase MCP returns the JWT and constructing `https://aaaplatform.vercel.app/sign/<token>` gives a working fallback URL — used today to recover Jadon's `6a9eaac0` contract without re-sending. **Latent risk noted (deferred):** Tiptap's Link extension default `validate` may strip non-URL hrefs like `{{signing_link}}` if the editor round-trips through `editor.getHTML()` on edit; today's bug was simpler (full body replacement) so this pathway wasn't exercised, but if a user edits the body without explicitly removing the link, the post-Tiptap-stripped body could lack the token. The new guards catch this case correctly (token-less body → guard fires); for a stronger fix, configure Tiptap's Link extension with a permissive `validate` inside the SendContractModal's email-body editor so `{{signing_link}}` survives the round-trip. See [[2026-05-07-build-15f-15g-signature-pad-and-send-guardrail]].

Stack: `react-pdf` ^10 (wraps pdfjs-dist) for in-browser rendering in editor + customer view; `pdf-lib` ^1.17 for server-side stamping. **Distinct from 67c1's `@react-pdf/renderer` stack** — that one builds PDFs from React; `pdf-lib` modifies existing PDF bytes; both libs ship together post-15d. Drag-from-palette UX (industry-standard DocuSign/PandaDoc pattern). Coords stored as PDF points top-left; `stamp-pdf.ts` translates to bottom-left for `pdf-lib` at draw time. - **[[build-15h-followup]] — Chrome `/sign/[token]` hang fix (email-iframe sandbox inheritance)** (2026-05-08 single focused session on Vanessa's MacBook Pro, `main` HEAD `d9f92ef` in sync with `origin/main`; one commit, one-line edit at `src/components/email-reader.tsx:62` adding `allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox` to the inbox iframe sandbox token list). Closes finding #4 — final 15h-deferred UX item. The in-app `/email` inbox rendered email body HTML inside `<iframe sandbox="allow-same-origin allow-popups">` with `<base target="_blank">` injected so every link opened a new tab; per HTML spec, popups from a sandboxed iframe inherit the parent's sandbox flag set unless `allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox` is also granted, so the new `/sign/[token]` tab inherited the missing `allow-scripts` and React/pdfjs scripts were blocked at parse time → 28× "Blocked script execution because document's frame is sandboxed and the 'allow-scripts' permission is not set" → SSR shell rendered but never hydrated → no PDF fetch ever attempted. Same console signature 15e fixed for a different cause (pdf.js fake-worker fallback iframe was sandboxed); this time the parent tab itself was sandboxed via inheritance — cause was upstream. **Diagnosis was the work; the fix was one token.** Three-context repro nailed it (incognito-paste OK, MCP-controlled tab in same Chrome profile OK with workerSrc + SW + cache state all healthy, click-from-email still hung — differentiator was the navigation path, not the URL or cache or login state). Eric's "logged in on Chrome but not on Safari?" hypothesis ruled out via proxy allowlist + service-role SSR + cross-origin PDF fetch + matcher-exempt worker. Live AAA-prod verification PASS via Eric clicking the contract link from `/email` after Vercel deploy, verbatim "it worked." Customer impact narrow — affects email clients that sandbox the rendered body (Gmail web, Outlook web, the in-app `/email` inbox); native mail clients (Apple Mail, Outlook desktop, mobile mail) don't, so most real-world signing flows would not have hit it. **All four 15h UX findings now closed.** Diagnosis fully controller-driven via `mcp__claude-in-chrome__*` (zero subagents); memorized the linkage to project memory `project_email_iframe_sandbox_popups.md` so future hardening on `<EmailBodyFrame>` doesn't re-break signing. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No DB migrations. No new tests. See [[2026-05-08-build-15h-followup-chrome-sign-sandbox]].

## Major shipped systems

- **Phase 1 platform** (Builds 1–10) — core jobs, customers, scheduling, photos. See [[build-1-10]], [[build-11]] (photo annotator).
- **Email** — inbox + attachments ([[build-12]], [[build-13]]); categories + body-pattern rules ([[build-27]], [[build-28]]).
- **Settings hub** (Build 14a–i) — company, appearance, statuses, auth, signatures, intake form, notifications, reports, export. See [[build-14a]]…[[build-14h-14i]].
- **Contracts** (Build 15a–c) — templates, remote signing, in-person/multi-signer/reminders. See [[build-15a]], [[build-15b]], [[build-15c]].
- **Accounting + QuickBooks** (Build 16a–d) — expenses, dashboard, QB connection, invoice/payment sync. See [[build-16a]], [[build-16b]], [[build-16c]], [[build-16d]].
- **Stripe payments** (Build 17a–c) — Connect + payment requests, public `/pay` page + emails, webhook + receipts/refunds + QB bridge. See [[build-17a]], [[build-17b]], [[build-17c]].
- **Jarvis AI assistant ecosystem** at `/jarvis` and `/api/jarvis`; knowledge base at `/settings/knowledge`. Four agents (Jarvis Core, R&D, Field Ops, Marketing) — see [[jarvis]]. Backed by **migrations 21, 23, 25a, 26b**. Marketing also has its own page at `/marketing` (Social Media + Chat tabs) — see [[build-26b]]. The Marketing **module** is the Jarvis Marketing sub-agent surfaced via a dedicated page.
- **Job UI iterations** — nav order ([[build-29]]), files section ([[build-30]]), insurance + photos redesign ([[build-31]]), soft-delete jobs + 30-day trash ([[build-66]]).
- **Multi-tenant infrastructure** — schema + backfill ([[build-18a]], migrations 42–54), RLS enforcement ([[build-18b]], migrations 55–60), workspace switcher ([[build-18c]], migrations 62/62b/63). `handle_new_user` trigger restoration follow-up: [[build-64]].
- **Capacitor iOS shell** — [[build-65a]]. Shipped to TestFlight as Nookleus. Live-bundle WebView per [[2026-04-26-capacitor-live-bundle]]; flips to bundled-static at 65e.
- **Knowledge vault** — scaffolding [[build-66a]], audit-first backfill [[build-66b]], skills [[build-66c]], per-machine Obsidian setup [[build-66d]]. All shipped 2026-04-29.
- **Estimates & Invoices Foundation** — [[build-67a]]. Estimate creation entry, full builder UI (sections + subsections + line items, dnd-kit reorder, Tiptap statements, AddItemDialog with library + custom tabs, TotalsPanel with markup/discount/tax + minimize), auto-save with retry/backoff/409 stale handling, read-only view, job-page integration. 67b adds estimate templates + invoice editor reusing the builder shell + estimate-to-invoice conversion. 67c1 adds PDF generation + Manager/Editor for presets + Export modal + retires `xactimate_code`; 67c2 will add send-via-email.
- **PDF Presets + Rendering + Export** — [[build-67c1]]. `pdf_presets` table with 8-toggle slim shape (markup/discount/tax/opening/closing/category-subtotals/code-col/notes-col) + `pdfs` private Storage bucket. `/settings/pdf-presets` Manager + Editor with default rotation. `@react-pdf/renderer`-based renderer (10 files: styles + types + html-to-pdf converter + 5 atomic components + 2 mode-specific components + 2 orchestrators + render dispatcher). POST `/api/{estimates,invoices}/[id]/pdf` routes render + upload + return signed URL. Export PDF button on builder + read-only views opens preset-picker modal → browser download. AFTER INSERT trigger on `organizations` seeds default presets for new orgs.

## Open threads

- **[[contracts-builder]] #67 Resolver design needs review before TDD loop continues.** `MergeFieldValueResolver` refactor must interpret `maps_to` strings (e.g., `"contact.first_name"` = join contacts via `job.contact_id` and return first_name) and preserve legacy slug resolution byte-for-byte against today's hardcoded `buildMergeFieldValues` paths. Risk: legacy templates regress if values don't match exactly. Walk through resolution-source dispatch design with Eric before writing the second resolver test.
- **[[contracts-builder]] #67 `form_config` backfill is risk-bearing.** Adding ~15 `merge_field_slug` entries to the seeded `form_config` row needs to be tested against AAA prod's actual current config (may have diverged from seed). Per `feedback_supabase_mcp_prod_migration_approval.md`, surface the JSON diff and ask "yes apply" before pushing.
- **[[contracts-builder]] #67 Working tree has 3 uncommitted files** that constitute the in-flight RegistryBuilder module — `src/lib/contracts/merge-field-registry.ts`, `src/lib/contracts/merge-field-registry.test.ts`, modified `src/lib/types.ts`. Next session should resume by running `npx vitest run src/lib/contracts/merge-field-registry.test.ts` (expect 9/9) before continuing.
- **Workplan Step 5 — Supabase dashboard auth-email templates + sender identity (manual work, on Eric).** Authentication → Email Templates → update Confirm signup, Magic Link, Reset Password, Invite user templates: replace "AAA Platform" / "AAA Disaster Recovery" copy with "Nookleus" + add the Nookleus lockup at the top via inline `<img>` HTML (`https://aaaplatform.vercel.app/nookleus-lockup-240w.png`). Authentication → Email Templates → Sender details: set sender name to "Nookleus"; leave sender email at the Supabase default until `nookleus.com` (or similar) is provisioned — do NOT route platform-auth mail through `@aaacontracting.com` (that's AAA tenant identity, not Nookleus platform identity).

- **iOS CI build failure on `2cfda55`.** The squash-merge to main triggered an App Store Connect CI run (build `11b1810d-7faf-4422-8cb7-a1147ecd6a12`) that errored. Separate from the web rebrand (iOS already shipped as Nookleus via [[build-65a]] build 3). Likely an iOS signing/CI config issue that needs a Mac session to triage. Web prod deploy is unaffected.

- **AAA workspace logo dependency on `company_settings.logo_path`.** The new dynamic sidebar logo (`6fd14cd`) renders AAA's logo IFF AAA has `logo_path` set in `company_settings`. If not, AAA users see "AAA Disaster Recovery" text + "ADR" initials in the collapsed-mode badge (regression vs the previous hardcoded `/logo.png`). Eric's fix: upload AAA's logo via Settings → Company once if it isn't already there. Verifying this is open.

- **Sidebar collapsed-mode badge for AAA went from "AAA" → "ADR".** The new initials-from-`company_name` algorithm computes "ADR" from "AAA Disaster Recovery". If Eric wants AAA to keep saying "AAA" (preserve the existing 3-letter brand mark), special-case orgs whose first word is all-uppercase to use the first word verbatim. Non-blocking aesthetic call.

- **Build 15h-followup polish carry-overs (non-blocking, optional).** (a) `<DownloadPdfButton>` sets `aria-busy` during the blob fetch but has no visible spinner — on a slow connection the user could double-tap (busy ref guards against duplicate fetches but provides no visual feedback); (b) error toast instead of `console.error` + last-ditch `window.location.href` fallback when fetch / Share fails for a non-Abort reason. Functional behavior is correct on the happy path; both are polish-only.

- **The autosave external-refresh re-baseline pattern (`22903f2`) is generic and may benefit other builders.** Any client component that takes a server-fetched entity prop, does `router.refresh()` on a dedicated mutation, AND maintains an autosave with `updated_at_snapshot` concurrency could hit the same stale-conflict 409 loop. Today only the estimate + invoice builders match that profile; future builders following the same pattern (template builders, contract editor) should adopt the same re-baseline effect. Worth flagging next time a new builder is added.

- **Build 15d Task 28 (§11 manual test pass) + Task 29 (cleanup) — CLOSED.** §11 12/12 resolved across the three 2026-05-06 test-pass sessions (10 PASS, 1 N/A); cleanup completed 2026-05-07 (3 test contracts + 6 test templates + 5 storage objects deleted from AAA + Test Co prod). Test-results doc at `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-06-build-15d-test-results.md` is the authoritative summary. Six bugs fixed inline (Bug 1 Untitled Template dupe `96eebeb`, Bug 2 PdfCanvas hardcoded scale `934883b`, Bugs 3+4 drop deselect + missing mergeFieldName `2a2bc32`, Bug 5 signature PNG MIME bucket migration, Bug 6 download wrong bucket `8f2411b`). Real customer validation: Jadon Daniels signed `WTR-2026-0020` 2026-05-07 15:14 UTC via the new flow. Storage caveat: ~595 KB orphan blobs in `contract-pdfs` may persist until Supabase storage GC runs (SQL escape hatch removes metadata rows but not backend blobs).

- **Build 15d Bug-2 candidate — `/api/settings/contract-templates/[id]/duplicate/route.ts:35` has the same dupe-name vulnerability as Bug 1.** The duplicate route does `name: \`${source.name} (Copy)\`` and will 500 on the second duplicate of the same source (`Foo (Copy)` already taken). Not blocking 15d's §11 pass directly (none of the 12 tests exercised duplicate-of-duplicate), but should be fixed before any further dupe-of-template work. Could share a `pickUniqueTemplateName(supabase, orgId, base)` helper with the create-empty fix.
- **Build 15d Task 25b — orphan-route porting (Build 15e in progress, 1 of 5 done).** `/api/contracts/[id]/sign/route.ts` (475 lines) and `/api/contracts/[id]/regenerate-pdf/route.ts` still exist post-15d; the five-feature unport list is now: ✅ (1) multi-signer next-signer email handoff — DONE 2026-05-07 in [[2026-05-07-build-15e]] (commit `4ed9d42`); reminder scheduling for the new signer was already wired via `schedule_first_reminder` RPC and is exercised end-to-end through the new path. ❌ (2) customer confirmation email with attached signed PDF, (3) internal confirmation email with attached signed PDF, (4) regenerate-signed-PDF endpoint. (Reminder scheduling for the *initial* send + the *next* signer is in-place; no further reminder work needed.) Once all four remaining items are shipped, delete the orphan routes + `src/lib/contracts/pdf.ts`. Net effect of leaving the remaining four unported: post-15d contracts go through the new flow successfully (sign + multi-signer handoff + stamp + persist) but skip the customer/internal confirmation emails and the regenerate endpoint entirely. Orphan routes stay reachable because no new code calls them, but they're dead weight.
- **Build 15d schema follow-up — relax `contracts.filled_content_html` NOT NULL constraint + RPC signature once 25b is done.** Task 27's draft-creation fix passes empty-string + sha256-of-empty as a placeholder for the still-NOT-NULL column; the `create_contract_with_signers` RPC still demands `p_filled_content_html text` + `p_filled_content_hash text`. Both can be relaxed to nullable in a future migration once Task 25b is done and no new contract writes meaningful HTML. Constants live in `src/lib/contracts/constants.ts` (`EMPTY_HTML` / `EMPTY_HTML_SHA256`) and would be deleted alongside the constraint relaxation.

- **Camera-preview + filesystem npm packages are in `node_modules` but not declared in `package.json`.** `b388106` added them to `ios/App/CapApp-SPM/Package.swift` directly, but `cap sync` strips them on every regeneration. Worth doing before CI/CD or scheduled iOS builds come into scope; not needed for occasional manual uploads.
- **Offline-stub workflow is fragile across fresh clones.** Both `out/*` and `ios/App/App/public/` are gitignored, but `cap sync` requires `out/index.html` to exist before it copies a stub into the iOS bundle. A fresh clone running cap sync without first creating the stub will produce an iOS bundle with no offline fallback. Two cleaner long-term options: (1) commit a minimal tracked `out/index.html` stub but keep the rest of `out/*` gitignored; (2) add an npm script (e.g. `prepare:ios`) that writes the stub before cap sync. Today's session created the stub by hand; it'll vanish on the next clone.
